SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Content], [t].[PublishedDate], [t].[AuthorId], [t].[Content0] AS [ContentComment], [a].[Name] AS [AuthorComment]
FROM (
    SELECT NULL AS [empty]
) AS [empty]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[AuthorId], [p].[Content], [p].[PublishedDate], [p].[Title], [c].[AuthorId] AS [AuthorId0], [c].[Content] AS [Content0]
    FROM [Post] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [Comment] AS [c] ON [p].[Id] = [c].[PostId]
    WHERE [p].[PublishedDate] IS NOT NULL AND ([c].[Available] = 1)
) AS [t] ON 1 = 1
INNER JOIN [Author] AS [a] ON [t].[AuthorId0] = [a].[Id]
ORDER BY [t].[PublishedDate] DESC
